4773<h3 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">

47741. What do we mean by "cookie"?</h3>

4775 </div>

4776

4777</div>

4778

4779<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-7e2133c elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="7e2133c" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">

4783<div class="elementor-text-editor elementor-clearfix">

4784

4785<p>

4786<strong>

4787In short:</strong>

4788</p>

4789

4790<p>

4791Cookies are small text files that are placed on your computer or mobile applications by websites that you visit. They are widely used in order to make websites work, and also to provide organizations some information on you and on your browsing activities.</p>

4792

4793<p>

4794<strong>

4795In detail: </strong>

4796</p>

4797

4798<p>

4799Cookies have several functions, such as allowing you to navigate efficiently on a website or a mobile application, remembering your choices and the goods and services you purchased. Thanks to cookies, we:</p>

4800

4801<ul>

4802

4803<li>

4804improve the knowledge we have of you and your interests;</li>

4805

4806<li>

4807offer you content specifically personalized for you (for example to remember the choice of language you have made on our site, or to show you advertisements that are tailored to your needs and interest).</li>

4808

4809</ul>

4810

4811<p>

4812<span lang="EN-US" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; user-select: text; -webkit-user-drag: none; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; color: #000000; text-align: justify; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 20.7px; font-family: Calibri, Calibri_EmbeddedFont, Calibri_MSFontService, sans-serif; font-variant-ligatures: none !important;" xml:lang="EN-US" data-contrast="auto">

4815similar to</span>

4816<span lang="EN-US" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; user-select: text; -webkit-user-drag: none; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; color: #000000; text-align: justify; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 20.7px; font-family: Calibri, Calibri_EmbeddedFont, Calibri_MSFontService, sans-serif; font-variant-ligatures: none !important;" xml:lang="EN-US" data-contrast="auto">

4817 cookies, such as scripts, pixels</span>

4818<span lang="EN-US" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; user-select: text; -webkit-user-drag: none; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; color: #000000; text-align: justify; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 20.7px; font-family: Calibri, Calibri_EmbeddedFont, Calibri_MSFontService, sans-serif; font-variant-ligatures: none !important;" xml:lang="EN-US" data-contrast="auto">
